<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́н</a> (3787)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">salon</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">reception room</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">salón</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>salon (fashionable shop or customer service), hairdressing salon
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́н</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:красота.html>красоты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>salón</b> krasoty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">beauty salon</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">массажный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">massažnyj <b>salón</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">massage parlour</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>show, exhibition
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авиационный.html>авиацио́нный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">aviaciónnyj <b>salón</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">air show</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:автомобильный.html>автомоби́льный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">avtomobílʹnyj <b>salón</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">motor show</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:демонстрационный.html>демонстрацио́нный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">demonstraciónnyj <b>salón</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">showroom</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>art gallery</li>
<li>lounge, waiting room
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́н</a></b> би́знес-кла́сса (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:аэропорт.html>аэропорту</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>salón</b> bíznes-klássa (v aeroportu)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">business/executive class lounge</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>cabin, passenger compartment
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́н</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:автомобиль.html>автомоби́ля</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>salón</b> avtomobílja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">inside of a car</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:салон.html>сало́н</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвого</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:класс.html>кла́сса</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> самолёте)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>salón</b> pérvovo klássa (v samoljóte)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">first class cabin/compartment</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>(reception with performing poets, musicians etc) salon</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> saloon</li></ol>

***сальный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сальный.html>са́льный</a> (19155)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сало.html>са́ло</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sálo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сальный.html>са́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sálʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)са́льнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)са́льней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> animal fat, lard
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сальный.html>са́льная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:железо.html>железа́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sálʹnaja</b> železá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fat gland</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tallow
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сальный.html>са́льная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свечка.html>све́чка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sálʹnaja</b> svéčka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tallow candle</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>containing a high percentage of fat <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. of an animal breed</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>left by fat <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. of a spot or mark</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>greasy</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:салют.html>салю́т</a> (11407)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in 1720. Via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Salut</i> or directly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">salut</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">salūs</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:салют.html>салю́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">saljút</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:салют.html>салю́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:салют.html>салю́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:салют.html>салю́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fireworks</li>
<li>salute</li></ol>

***сам.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сам.html>сам</a> (72)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*samъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*SomHós</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сам.html>сам</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sam</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>neuter</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сам.html>само́</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сам.html>сама́</a></b>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сам.html>са́ми</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">definitive pronoun<span class="ib-comma">,</span> emphatic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> self, -self
<dl><dd><ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сам.html>сам</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́дел</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>sam</b> éto vídel</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I saw it myself.</span></dd></dl></div></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:самбо.html>са́мбо</a> (23473)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Acronym of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самооборона.html>самооборо́на</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:самозащита.html>самозащи́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оружие.html>ору́жия</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">samooboróna/samozaščíta bez orúžija</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">self-defense without weapons</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самбо.html>са́мбо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sámbo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:саммит.html>са́ммит</a> (21908)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">summit</i>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:саммит.html>са́ммит</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sámmit</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:саммит.html>са́ммита</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:саммит.html>са́ммиты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:саммит.html>са́ммитов</a></b>)

***самовар.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:самовар.html>самова́р</a> (5486)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">само-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">samo-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">self-</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + a deverbal form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:варить.html>вари́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">varítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to boil</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самовар.html>самова́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">samovár</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самовар.html>самова́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самовар.html>самова́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самовар.html>самова́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>samovar <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a large coal- or woodfired metal urn with a spigot for boiling water for tea</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">самово́л(ие)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">samovól(ije)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="неодобрительное">неодобр.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:самовольный.html>самово́льные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:действие.html>де́йствия</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:идущий.html>иду́щие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вразрез.html>вразре́з</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:план.html>пла́ном</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:норма.html>но́рмой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> т. п. <span class="example-fullblock example-absent-block"><ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самолюбие.html>самолю́бие</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">samoljúbije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самолюбивый.html>самолюби́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">samoljubívyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)самолюби́вее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)самолюби́вей</b>)
